38  public class IBM1383_OLD
39      extends Charset
40      implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
41  {
42  
43      public IBM1383_OLD() {
44          super("x-IBM1383-Old", null);
45      }
46  
47      public String historicalName() {
48          return "Cp1383";
49      }
50  
51      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
52          return (cs instanceof IBM1383);
53      }
54  
55      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
56          return new Decoder(this);
57      }
58  
59      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
60          return new Encoder(this);
61      }
62  
63      public String getDecoderSingleByteMappings() {
64          return Decoder.byteToCharTable;
65      }
66  
67      public String getDecoderMappingTableG1() {
68          return Decoder.mappingTableG1;
69      }
70  
71      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
72          return Encoder.index1;
73  
74      }
75      public String getEncoderIndex2() {
76          return Encoder.index2;
77  
78      }
79      public String getEncoderIndex2a() {
80          return Encoder.index2a;
81      }
